 2
 After 7 o'clock in the evening, if the working hour is fixed, then the company will be responsible for safety
 3
 It would be necessary to seek the consent of the employee before taking overtime
 4
 The maximum overtime in a month will be 125 hours instead of 100 hours
 5
 The definition of family will be expanded
 6

 7

 8
